            description "NETWORK QoS POLICY Ingress classification,Egress remarking "
            ingress
                default-action fc be profile in
                dscp be fc be profile out
                dscp cs1 fc ef profile in
                dscp cs2 fc ef profile in
                dscp cs3 fc ef profile in
                dscp cs4 fc h2 profile in
                dscp cs5 fc ef profile in
                dscp nc1 fc h2 profile in
                dscp nc2 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 0 fc be profile out
                lsp-exp 1 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 2 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 3 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 4 fc h2 profile in
                lsp-exp 5 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 6 fc h2 profile in
                lsp-exp 7 fc ef profile in
            exit
            egress
                remarking
                fc ef
                    dscp-in-profile cs5
                    dscp-out-profile cs5
                exit
                fc h2
                    dscp-in-profile cs4
                    dscp-out-profile cs4
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit

        bgp
            multipath 8
            ibgp-multipath
            local-as 64741
            router-id 61.175.0.4
            next-hop-resolution
                use-bgp-routes
            exit
            group "iBGP"
                family vpn-ipv4
                peer-as 64741
                local-address 61.175.1.2
                neighbor 61.153.112.13
                exit
                neighbor 61.175.1.254
                exit
            exit
            group "pgCR"
                family ipv4
                keepalive 60
                hold-time 180
                type internal
                preference 200
                export "rpSET_COMM_OUT" 
                peer-as 64741
                local-address 61.175.0.4
                neighbor 61.175.0.1
                    description "uT:NB-NB-YSN-CR-1.MAN.NE5000E"
                exit
                neighbor 61.175.0.2
                    description "uT:NB-NB-ESN-CR-1.MAN.NE5000E"
                exit
            exit
            group "pgCRv6"
                family ipv6
                keepalive 60
                hold-time 180
                damping
                type internal
                preference 200
                import "rpFROMCR_INv6" 
                export "rpStaticToBGPv6" "rpSET_COMM_OUTv6" 
                graceful-restart
                    stale-routes-time 10
                exit
                local-as 64741
                peer-as 64741
                local-address 240e:1c:2013:1000::1
                neighbor 240e:1c:2011:1000::1
